found\u003c/strong\u003e: Ubuntu 24.04 doesn't include \u003ccode\u003etoolbox\u003c/code\u003e in repos. Optimal Ubuntu 24.04 Setup Roadmap for GMKTEC EVO-X2 (Ryzen AI Max+ 395)","","Based on your research, here's the step-by-step roadmap optimized for ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA and hipBLASlt:","","## Phase 1: BIOS Configuration (BEFORE OS Installation)","","**Step 1.1: Configure GPU Memory**","- Set GART (Graphics Aperture Remapping Table) to **512MB minimum**","- Navigate to: Integrated Graphics → UMA Frame Buffer Size → 512MB","- If available: Device Manager → AMD CBS → NBIO Common Options → GFX Configuration → Set as needed","","**Step 1.2: Disable IOMMU**","- Find IOMMU setting in BIOS","- Set to **Disabled** (provides ~6% memory read improvement)","- Only enable if you need VFIO/GPU passthrough later","","**Step 1.3: Set Power Mode**","- Configure to **85W** (optimal balance: +19% vs 55W, avoids diminishing returns of 120W)","","## Phase 2: Ubuntu 24.04 Base Installation","","**Step 2.1: Install Ubuntu 24.04**","- Use Ubuntu 24.04 LTS Desktop or Server","- During installation, use default partitioning or your preferred scheme","- Complete initial setup (user account, timezone, etc.)","","**Step 2.2: Initial System Update**","```bash","sudo apt update \u0026\u0026 sudo apt upgrade -y","```","","## Phase 3: Critical Kernel Configuration","","**Step 3.1: Install Mainline Kernel Tool**","```bash","sudo add-apt-repository ppa:cappelikan/ppa -y","sudo apt update","sudo apt install mainline -y","```","","**Step 3.2: Install Kernel 6.16.9 or Later**","```bash","# Check available kernels","sudo mainline --list | grep \"6.1[6-9]\\|6.2\"","","# Install latest stable (e.g., 6.16.9 or 6.17.x)","sudo mainline --install 6.16.9","","# Or manually download if needed","# sudo mainline --install-latest","```","","**Step 3.3: Install Latest Firmware**","```bash","sudo apt install linux-firmware -y","# For bleeding edge (optional):","# sudo add-apt-repository ppa:firmware-testing/ppa -y","# sudo apt update \u0026\u0026 sudo apt install linux-firmware -y","```","","**Step 3.4: Configure GRUB Boot Parameters**","","Edit `/etc/default/grub`:","```bash","sudo nano /etc/default/grub","```","","Modify the `GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT` line to include:","```","GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT=\"quiet splash amd_iommu=off amdgpu.gttsize=131072 ttm.pages_limit=31457280\"","```","","Update GRUB and regenerate initramfs:","```bash","sudo update-grub","sudo update-initramfs -u -k all","```","","**Step 3.5: Create AMD GPU Modprobe Configuration**","","Create `/etc/modprobe.d/amdgpu_llm_optimized.conf`:","```bash","sudo nano /etc/modprobe.d/amdgpu_llm_optimized.conf","```","","Add the following content:","```bash","# Legacy compatibility setting","options amdgpu gttsize=122800","","# Primary GTT configuration - 120 GiB allocation","options ttm pages_limit=31457280","","# Pre-allocate memory pool to reduce fragmentation","# This memory becomes permanently unavailable to the system","# Set equal to pages_limit for maximum performance","options ttm page_pool_size=31457280","","# Optional: Increase fragment size for larger allocations","# Uncomment if experiencing fragmentation issues","# options amdgpu vm_fragment_size=8","```","","Update initramfs:","```bash","sudo update-initramfs -u -k all","```","","**Step 3.6: Reboot to New Kernel**","```bash","sudo reboot","```","","After reboot, verify kernel:","```bash","uname -r  # Should show 6.16.9 or later","```","","## Phase 4: GPU Access Configuration (Critical for Ubuntu)","","**Step 4.1: Create udev Rules for GPU Access**","","Create `/etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules`:","```bash","sudo bash -c 'cat \u003e /etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules \u003c\u003c EOF","SUBSYSTEM==\"kfd\", GROUP=\"render\", MODE=\"0666\", OPTIONS+=\"last_rule\"","SUBSYSTEM==\"drm\", KERNEL==\"card[0-9]*\", GROUP=\"render\", MODE=\"0666\", OPTIONS+=\"last_rule\"","SUBSYSTEM==\"drm\", KERNEL==\"renderD[0-9]*\", GROUP=\"render\", MODE=\"0666\", OPTIONS+=\"last_rule\"","EOF'","```","","**IMPORTANT:** The `renderD[0-9]*` rule is critical for ROCm access. Without it, you'll get `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` errors when running `rocminfo`.","","Reload udev rules:","```bash","sudo udevadm control --reload-rules","sudo udevadm trigger","```","","Verify permissions:","```bash","ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/","# All devices should show MODE 0666 (crw-rw-rw-)","```","","**Step 4.2: Add User to GPU Groups**","```bash","sudo usermod -aG video,render $USER","```","","## Phase 5: System Performance Optimization","","**Step 5.1: Install and Configure tuned Daemon**","```bash","sudo apt install tuned -y","sudo systemctl enable --now tuned","sudo tuned-adm profile accelerator-performance","```","","Verify activation:","```bash","tuned-adm active  # Should show \"accelerator-performance\"","```","","This provides **+5-8% prompt processing performance improvement**.","","## Phase 6: Container Environment Setup","","**Step 6.1: Install Podman and Distrobox**","","```bash","# Install Podman","sudo apt install podman -y","","# Install Distrobox (toolbox is not available in Ubuntu repos)","curl -s https://raw.githubusercontent.com/89luca89/distrobox/main/install | sudo sh","```","","**NOTE:** Ubuntu 24.04 does not include `toolbox` in its repositories. We use **Distrobox** instead, which is fully compatible with Podman and provides the same functionality. All `toolbox` commands should be replaced with `distrobox` commands.","","**Step 6.2: Configure Podman for GPU Access**","","Ensure your user can run containers:","```bash","sudo loginctl enable-linger $USER","```","","Verify installations:","```bash","podman --version      # Should show 4.9.3 or later","distrobox --version   # Should show 1.8.2.0 or later","```","","## Phase 7: ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA Setup","","**Step 7.1: Create ROCm 7 RC Container with rocWMMA**","","```bash","distrobox create llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma \\","  --image docker.io/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes:rocm-7rc-rocwmma \\","  --additional-flags \"--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render --group-add sudo --security-opt seccomp=unconfined\"","```","","**NOTE:** The command syntax differs from `toolbox`:","- Use `--additional-flags` instead of `--` separator","- Container creation may take a few minutes on first run","","**Step 7.2: Enter the Container**","```bash","distrobox enter llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma","```","","Verify you're inside the container - you should see ROCm tools available:","```bash","rocm-smi          # Should show your GPU","rocminfo | head   # Should display HSA system info","```","","## Phase 8: Verification and Testing","","**Step 8.1: Verify GPU Memory Visibility**","","On host system:","```bash","# Check all memory info","for file in /sys/class/drm/card*/device/mem_info*; do","  echo \"$file: $(cat $file)\";","done","```","","**Expected values for Strix Halo APU:**","- `mem_info_vram_total`: 1073741824 bytes (1 GB - display framebuffer)","- `mem_info_gtt_total`: 137438953472 bytes (128 GB - unified compute memory)","","**IMPORTANT:** For APUs with unified memory, the **GTT** (Graphics Translation Table) is what matters for LLM inference, not VRAM. This is normal and correct.","","Inside ROCm container:","```bash","# Check ROCm visibility","rocminfo | grep -A100 'Agent 2' | grep -A50 'Pool Info'","","# Expected: Should show ~120GB in Pool 1 and Pool 2","```","","If you get `HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES`, verify:","```bash","# Check device permissions (should be 0666)","ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/renderD128","# Fix if needed - see Step 4.1 udev rules","```","","**Step 8.2: Test ROCm Functionality**","```bash","# Inside container","rocm-smi","","# Should detect your gfx1151 GPU","```","","**Step 8.3: Verify hipBLASlt Environment**","```bash","# Inside container","echo $ROCBLAS_USE_HIPBLASLT  # Should be \"1\"","```","","## Phase 9: Build llama.cpp with rocWMMA","","**Step 9.0: Install Build Dependencies**","","The ROCm container is based on Fedora and doesn't include build tools by default. Install them first:","","```bash","# Inside the container","sudo dnf install -y cmake gcc-c++ git libcurl-devel python3-pip","```","","This will install:","- `cmake` - Build system generator","- `gcc-c++` - C++ compiler","- `git` - Version control (for cloning llama.cpp)","- `libcurl-devel` - CURL library (required by llama.cpp)","","**Step 9.1: Clone and Build llama.cpp**","","Inside the ROCm container:","```bash","cd ~","git clone https://github.com/ggerganov/llama.cpp.git","cd llama.cpp","","# Build with rocWMMA support","cmake -B build -S . \\","  -DGGML_HIP=ON \\","  -DAMDGPU_TARGETS=\"gfx1151\" \\","  -DGGML_HIP_ROCWMMA_FATTN=ON","","cmake --build build --config Release -j$(nproc)","```","","**NOTE:** The build process will take several minutes. You'll see compilation progress for GPU kernels and CPU code.","","**Step 9.2: Install Build**","```bash","# Binaries will be in build/bin/","ls -lh build/bin/","```","","## Phase 10: Download Models and Test","","**Step 10.1: Set Up Model Directory**","```bash","# Outside container (in home directory to persist across container updates)","mkdir -p ~/models","cd ~/models","```","","**Step 10.2: Download a Test Model**","```bash","# Inside container","# Install HuggingFace CLI if not already available","pip install \"huggingface-hub[cli]\" hf-transfer","","# Enable fast downloads","export HF_HUB_ENABLE_HF_TRANSFER=1","","# Download a model (example: Llama 2 7B)","hf download TheBloke/Llama-2-7B-GGUF llama-2-7b.Q4_K_M.gguf --local-dir ~/models","```","```","","**Step 10.3: Run Inference Test**","```bash","cd ~/llama.cpp","","# CRITICAL: Always use --no-mmap with GPU backends on Strix Halo","./build/bin/llama-cli \\","  -m ~/models/llama-2-7b.Q4_K_M.gguf \\","  --no-mmap \\","  -ngl 99 \\","  -p \"Tell me about AMD Strix Halo processors\" \\","  -n 128","```","","## Phase 11: Performance Validation","","**Step 11.1: Run Benchmark**","```bash","cd ~/llama.cpp","","# Benchmark prompt processing at 512 tokens","./build/bin/llama-bench \\","  -m ~/models/llama-2-7b.Q4_K_M.gguf \\","  -mmp 0 \\","  -ngl 99 \\","  -p 512 \\","  -n 128","```","","**NOTE:** `llama-bench` uses `-mmp 0` (or `--mmap 0`) to disable mmap, not `--no-mmap` like `llama-cli`.","","**Step 11.2: Monitor GPU Utilization**","```bash","# In another terminal, inside container","watch -n 1 rocm-smi","```","","## Additional Recommendations","","### For Multiple Backend Testing","","**Create Vulkan Containers (Optional)**","```bash","# RADV (most stable)","distrobox create llama-vulkan-radv \\","  --image docker.io/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes:vulkan-radv \\","  --additional-flags \"--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render\"","","# AMDVLK (fastest prompt processing)","distrobox create llama-vulkan-amdvlk \\","  --image docker.io/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes:vulkan-amdvlk \\","  --additional-flags \"--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render\"","```","","### Useful Tools","","**Install VRAM Estimator**","```bash","# Clone helper scripts","git clone https://github.com/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes.git ~/strix-tools","```","","**Refresh Containers Script**","```bash","cd ~/strix-tools","./refresh-toolboxes.sh llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma","```","","## Critical Reminders","","1. **Always use `--no-mmap`** flag with llama.cpp on GPU backends","2. **Always use `--ngl 99`** (or 999) to offload all layers to GPU","3. **Store models in ~/models** (outside containers) to persist across updates","4. **Never use Ollama** - it lacks proper Vulkan/AMD support","5. **Kernel 6.16.9+** is critical for \u003e15GB VRAM access","6. **Don't change VRAM allocation at OS level** after BIOS setup","7. **Set `ROCBLAS_USE_HIPBLASLT=1`** environment variable (already set in kyuz0 containers)","","## Performance Expectations","","- **Llama-2-7B**: ~50-52 tokens/second (similar to Apple M4 Max)","- **Prompt processing with rocWMMA**: 2× faster than Vulkan at BF16","- **Long context (8K+ tokens)**: ROCm rocWMMA excels (51 t/s vs Vulkan's 32 t/s)","- **Memory bandwidth**: ~212 GB/s internal, ~84 GB/s CPU-to-GPU","","## Troubleshooting Quick Reference","","### Ubuntu-Specific Issues","","- **`toolbox` package not found**: Ubuntu 24.04 doesn't include `toolbox` in repos. Use `distrobox` instead (see Phase 6)","- **`HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES` when running `rocminfo`**: Missing renderD udev rule. Ensure `/etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules` includes the `renderD[0-9]*` rule (see Step 4.1), then reload with `sudo udevadm control --reload-rules \u0026\u0026 sudo udevadm trigger`","- **Container can't access GPU**: Verify device permissions with `ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/`. All should be `0666` (crw-rw-rw-)","","### Build Issues in Container","","- **`cmake: command not found`**: The ROCm container doesn't include build tools. Install them with `sudo dnf install -y cmake gcc-c++ git libcurl-devel` (see Step 9.0)","- **`Could NOT find CURL` error during cmake**: Install libcurl-devel with `sudo dnf install -y libcurl-devel`","- **Container uses `dnf` not `apt`**: The ROCm container is Fedora-based. Use `dnf` for package management, not `apt`","","### llama.cpp Runtime Issues","","- **`error: invalid argument: --ngl`**: Use `-ngl` (single dash) not `--ngl` (double dash) for GPU layer offloading","- **`error: invalid parameter for argument: --no-mmap`** (llama-bench): Use `-mmp 0` or `--mmap 0` instead. The `--no-mmap` flag only works with `llama-cli`, not `llama-bench`","- **`hf: command not found`**: The HuggingFace CLI changed to `hf download` instead of `huggingface-cli download`. If using pyenv, use full path: `~/.pyenv/versions/3.14.0/bin/hf`","- **Square brackets error in zsh** (`huggingface-hub[cli]`): Quote the package name: `pip install \"huggingface-hub[cli]\"`","","### General Issues","","- **Permission denied on GPU**: Check udev rules in Phase 4 and verify user is in `video` and `render` groups","- **Only 15.5GB VRAM visible**: Upgrade kernel to 6.16.9+","- **Slow model loading**: Add `--no-mmap` flag","- **ROCm crashes**: Try Vulkan RADV backend instead","- **Poor performance**: Verify `tuned-adm active` shows accelerator-performance","- **Confused about VRAM vs GTT**: For APUs, GTT (128GB) is what matters for compute, not VRAM (1GB). This is normal and expected.","","## Next Steps After Setup","","Once you have completed this roadmap and verified that everything works:","","1. **Benchmark multiple backends** (ROCm 7 RC rocWMMA, Vulkan RADV, Vulkan AMDVLK) with your specific workloads","2. **Test with different model sizes** to find optimal configurations for your 120GB VRAM","3. **Explore long-context scenarios** where ROCm rocWMMA significantly outperforms Vulkan","4. **Monitor kernel updates** as gfx1151 support continues to mature","5. **Consider TheRock nightly builds** for bleeding-edge performance improvements","","This roadmap gives you a production-ready setup for ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA and hipBLASlt on your GMKTEC EVO-X2. The container-based approach ensures reproducibility and easy updates as ROCm support for gfx1151 continues actions</span></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="BlobViewContent-module__blobContentWrapper__JS0W6"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="BlobContent-module__blobContentSection__VOgZq BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true" containertiming="hpc"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Optimal Ubuntu 24.04 Setup Roadmap for GMKTEC EVO-X2 (Ryzen AI Max+ 395)</h1><a id="user-content-optimal-ubuntu-2404-setup-roadmap-for-gmktec-evo-x2-ryzen-ai-max-395" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Optimal Ubuntu 24.04 Setup Roadmap for GMKTEC EVO-X2 (Ryzen AI Max+ 395)" href="#optimal-ubuntu-2404-setup-roadmap-for-gmktec-evo-x2-ryzen-ai-max-395"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Based on your research, here's the step-by-step roadmap optimized for ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA and hipBLASlt:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 1: BIOS Configuration (BEFORE OS Installation)</h2><a id="user-content-phase-1-bios-configuration-before-os-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 1: BIOS Configuration (BEFORE OS Installation)" href="#phase-1-bios-configuration-before-os-installation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 1.1: Configure GPU Memory</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Set GART (Graphics Aperture Remapping Table) to <strong>512MB minimum</strong></li>
<li>Navigate to: Integrated Graphics → UMA Frame Buffer Size → 512MB</li>
<li>If available: Device Manager → AMD CBS → NBIO Common Options → GFX Configuration → Set as needed</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 1.2: Disable IOMMU</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Find IOMMU setting in BIOS</li>
<li>Set to <strong>Disabled</strong> (provides ~6% memory read improvement)</li>
<li>Only enable if you need VFIO/GPU passthrough later</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 1.3: Set Power Mode</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Configure to <strong>85W</strong> (optimal balance: +19% vs 55W, avoids diminishing returns of 120W)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 2: Ubuntu 24.04 Base Installation</h2><a id="user-content-phase-2-ubuntu-2404-base-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 2: Ubuntu 24.04 Base Installation" href="#phase-2-ubuntu-2404-base-installation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 2.1: Install Ubuntu 24.04</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use Ubuntu 24.04 LTS Desktop or Server</li>
<li>During installation, use default partitioning or your preferred scheme</li>
<li>Complete initial setup (user account, timezone, etc.)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 2.2: Initial System Update</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo apt update &amp;&amp; sudo apt upgrade -y"><pre>sudo apt update <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> sudo apt upgrade -y</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 3: Critical Kernel Configuration</h2><a id="user-content-phase-3-critical-kernel-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 3: Critical Kernel Configuration" href="#phase-3-critical-kernel-configuration"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3.1: Install Mainline Kernel Tool</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo add-apt-repository ppa:cappelikan/ppa -y
sudo apt update
sudo apt install mainline -y"><pre>sudo add-apt-repository ppa:cappelikan/ppa -y
sudo apt update
sudo apt install mainline -y</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3.2: Install Kernel 6.16.9 or Later</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Check available kernels
sudo mainline --list | grep &quot;6.1[6-9]\|6.2&quot;

# Install latest stable (e.g., 6.16.9 or 6.17.x)
sudo mainline --install 6.16.9

# Or manually download if needed
# sudo mainline --install-latest"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Check available kernels</span>
sudo mainline --list <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>6.1[6-9]\|6.2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install latest stable (e.g., 6.16.9 or 6.17.x)</span>
sudo mainline --install 6.16.9

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Or manually download if needed</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> sudo mainline --install-latest</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3.3: Install Latest Firmware</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo apt install linux-firmware -y
# For bleeding edge (optional):
# sudo add-apt-repository ppa:firmware-testing/ppa -y
# sudo apt update &amp;&amp; sudo apt install linux-firmware -y"><pre>sudo apt install linux-firmware -y
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For bleeding edge (optional):</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> sudo add-apt-repository ppa:firmware-testing/ppa -y</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> sudo apt update &amp;&amp; sudo apt install linux-firmware -y</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3.4: Configure GRUB Boot Parameters</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Edit <code>/etc/default/grub</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo nano /etc/default/grub"><pre>sudo nano /etc/default/grub</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Modify the <code>GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT</code> line to include:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT=&quot;quiet splash amd_iommu=off amdgpu.gttsize=131072 ttm.pages_limit=31457280&quot;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>GRUB_CMDLINE_LINUX_DEFAULT="quiet splash amd_iommu=off amdgpu.gttsize=131072 ttm.pages_limit=31457280"
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Update GRUB and regenerate initramfs:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo update-grub
sudo update-initramfs -u -k all"><pre>sudo update-grub
sudo update-initramfs -u -k all</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3.5: Create AMD GPU Modprobe Configuration</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Create <code>/etc/modprobe.d/amdgpu_llm_optimized.conf</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo nano /etc/modprobe.d/amdgpu_llm_optimized.conf"><pre>sudo nano /etc/modprobe.d/amdgpu_llm_optimized.conf</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Add the following content:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Legacy compatibility setting
options amdgpu gttsize=122800

# Primary GTT configuration - 120 GiB allocation
options ttm pages_limit=31457280

# Pre-allocate memory pool to reduce fragmentation
# This memory becomes permanently unavailable to the system
# Set equal to pages_limit for maximum performance
options ttm page_pool_size=31457280

# Optional: Increase fragment size for larger allocations
# Uncomment if experiencing fragmentation issues
# options amdgpu vm_fragment_size=8"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Legacy compatibility setting</span>
options amdgpu gttsize=122800

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Primary GTT configuration - 120 GiB allocation</span>
options ttm pages_limit=31457280

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Pre-allocate memory pool to reduce fragmentation</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> This memory becomes permanently unavailable to the system</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Set equal to pages_limit for maximum performance</span>
options ttm page_pool_size=31457280

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Optional: Increase fragment size for larger allocations</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Uncomment if experiencing fragmentation issues</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> options amdgpu vm_fragment_size=8</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Update initramfs:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo update-initramfs -u -k all"><pre>sudo update-initramfs -u -k all</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3.6: Reboot to New Kernel</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo reboot"><pre>sudo reboot</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">After reboot, verify kernel:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uname -r  # Should show 6.16.9 or later"><pre>uname -r  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should show 6.16.9 or later</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 4: GPU Access Configuration (Critical for Ubuntu)</h2><a id="user-content-phase-4-gpu-access-configuration-critical-for-ubuntu" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 4: GPU Access Configuration (Critical for Ubuntu)" href="#phase-4-gpu-access-configuration-critical-for-ubuntu"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 4.1: Create udev Rules for GPU Access</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Create <code>/etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo bash -c 'cat &gt; /etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules &lt;&lt; EOF
SUBSYSTEM==&quot;kfd&quot;, GROUP=&quot;render&quot;, MODE=&quot;0666&quot;, OPTIONS+=&quot;last_rule&quot;
SUBSYSTEM==&quot;drm&quot;, KERNEL==&quot;card[0-9]*&quot;, GROUP=&quot;render&quot;, MODE=&quot;0666&quot;, OPTIONS+=&quot;last_rule&quot;
SUBSYSTEM==&quot;drm&quot;, KERNEL==&quot;renderD[0-9]*&quot;, GROUP=&quot;render&quot;, MODE=&quot;0666&quot;, OPTIONS+=&quot;last_rule&quot;
EOF'"><pre>sudo bash -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>cat &gt; /etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules &lt;&lt; EOF</span>
<span class="pl-s">SUBSYSTEM=="kfd", GROUP="render", MODE="0666", OPTIONS+="last_rule"</span>
<span class="pl-s">SUBSYSTEM=="drm", KERNEL=="card[0-9]*", GROUP="render", MODE="0666", OPTIONS+="last_rule"</span>
<span class="pl-s">SUBSYSTEM=="drm", KERNEL=="renderD[0-9]*", GROUP="render", MODE="0666", OPTIONS+="last_rule"</span>
<span class="pl-s">EOF<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IMPORTANT:</strong> The <code>renderD[0-9]*</code> rule is critical for ROCm access. Without it, you'll get <code>HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES</code> errors when running <code>rocminfo</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Reload udev rules:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo udevadm control --reload-rules
sudo udevadm trigger"><pre>sudo udevadm control --reload-rules
sudo udevadm trigger</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Verify permissions:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/
# All devices should show MODE 0666 (crw-rw-rw-)"><pre>ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> All devices should show MODE 0666 (crw-rw-rw-)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 4.2: Add User to GPU Groups</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo usermod -aG video,render $USER"><pre>sudo usermod -aG video,render <span class="pl-smi">$USER</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 5: System Performance Optimization</h2><a id="user-content-phase-5-system-performance-optimization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 5: System Performance Optimization" href="#phase-5-system-performance-optimization"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 5.1: Install and Configure tuned Daemon</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo apt install tuned -y
sudo systemctl enable --now tuned
sudo tuned-adm profile accelerator-performance"><pre>sudo apt install tuned -y
sudo systemctl <span class="pl-c1">enable</span> --now tuned
sudo tuned-adm profile accelerator-performance</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Verify activation:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="tuned-adm active  # Should show &quot;accelerator-performance&quot;"><pre>tuned-adm active  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should show "accelerator-performance"</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This provides <strong>+5-8% prompt processing performance improvement</strong>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 6: Container Environment Setup</h2><a id="user-content-phase-6-container-environment-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 6: Container Environment Setup" href="#phase-6-container-environment-setup"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 6.1: Install Podman and Distrobox</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Install Podman
sudo apt install podman -y

# Install Distrobox (toolbox is not available in Ubuntu repos)
curl -s https://raw.githubusercontent.com/89luca89/distrobox/main/install | sudo sh"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install Podman</span>
sudo apt install podman -y

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install Distrobox (toolbox is not available in Ubuntu repos)</span>
curl -s https://raw.githubusercontent.com/89luca89/distrobox/main/install <span class="pl-k">|</span> sudo sh</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE:</strong> Ubuntu 24.04 does not include <code>toolbox</code> in its repositories. We use <strong>Distrobox</strong> instead, which is fully compatible with Podman and provides the same functionality. All <code>toolbox</code> commands should be replaced with <code>distrobox</code> commands.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 6.2: Configure Podman for GPU Access</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Ensure your user can run containers:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo loginctl enable-linger $USER"><pre>sudo loginctl enable-linger <span class="pl-smi">$USER</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Verify installations:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="podman --version      # Should show 4.9.3 or later
distrobox --version   # Should show 1.8.2.0 or later"><pre>podman --version      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should show 4.9.3 or later</span>
distrobox --version   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should show 1.8.2.0 or later</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 7: ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA Setup</h2><a id="user-content-phase-7-rocm-7-rc-with-rocwmma-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 7: ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA Setup" href="#phase-7-rocm-7-rc-with-rocwmma-setup"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 7.1: Create ROCm 7 RC Container with rocWMMA</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="distrobox create llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma \
  --image docker.io/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes:rocm-7rc-rocwmma \
  --additional-flags &quot;--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render --group-add sudo --security-opt seccomp=unconfined&quot;"><pre>distrobox create llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma \
  --image docker.io/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes:rocm-7rc-rocwmma \
  --additional-flags <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render --group-add sudo --security-opt seccomp=unconfined<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE:</strong> The command syntax differs from <code>toolbox</code>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use <code>--additional-flags</code> instead of <code>--</code> separator</li>
<li>Container creation may take a few minutes on first run</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 7.2: Enter the Container</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="distrobox enter llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma"><pre>distrobox enter llama-rocm-7rc-rocwmma</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Verify you're inside the container - you should see ROCm tools available:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="rocm-smi          # Should show your GPU
rocminfo | head   # Should display HSA system info"><pre>rocm-smi          <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should show your GPU</span>
rocminfo <span class="pl-k">|</span> head   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should display HSA system info</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 8: Verification and Testing</h2><a id="user-content-phase-8-verification-and-testing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 8: Verification and Testing" href="#phase-8-verification-and-testing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 8.1: Verify GPU Memory Visibility</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">On host system:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Check all memory info
for file in /sys/class/drm/card*/device/mem_info*; do
  echo &quot;$file: $(cat $file)&quot;;
done"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Check all memory info</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">file</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> /sys/class/drm/card<span class="pl-k">*</span>/device/mem_info<span class="pl-k">*</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$file</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>cat <span class="pl-smi">$file</span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Expected values for Strix Halo APU:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>mem_info_vram_total</code>: 1073741824 bytes (1 GB - display framebuffer)</li>
<li><code>mem_info_gtt_total</code>: 137438953472 bytes (128 GB - unified compute memory)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IMPORTANT:</strong> For APUs with unified memory, the <strong>GTT</strong> (Graphics Translation Table) is what matters for LLM inference, not VRAM. This is normal and correct.</p>
<p dir="auto">Inside ROCm container:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Check ROCm visibility
rocminfo | grep -A100 'Agent 2' | grep -A50 'Pool Info'

# Expected: Should show ~120GB in Pool 1 and Pool 2"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Check ROCm visibility</span>
rocminfo <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -A100 <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Agent 2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -A50 <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Pool Info<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Expected: Should show ~120GB in Pool 1 and Pool 2</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If you get <code>HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES</code>, verify:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Check device permissions (should be 0666)
ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/renderD128
# Fix if needed - see Step 4.1 udev rules"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Check device permissions (should be 0666)</span>
ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/renderD128
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Fix if needed - see Step 4.1 udev rules</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 8.2: Test ROCm Functionality</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Inside container
rocm-smi

# Should detect your gfx1151 GPU"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Inside container</span>
rocm-smi

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should detect your gfx1151 GPU</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 8.3: Verify hipBLASlt Environment</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Inside container
echo $ROCBLAS_USE_HIPBLASLT  # Should be &quot;1&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Inside container</span>
<span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-smi">$ROCBLAS_USE_HIPBLASLT</span>  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should be "1"</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 9: Build llama.cpp with rocWMMA</h2><a id="user-content-phase-9-build-llamacpp-with-rocwmma" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 9: Build llama.cpp with rocWMMA" href="#phase-9-build-llamacpp-with-rocwmma"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 9.0: Install Build Dependencies</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The ROCm container is based on Fedora and doesn't include build tools by default. Install them first:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Inside the container
sudo dnf install -y cmake gcc-c++ git libcurl-devel python3-pip"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Inside the container</span>
sudo dnf install -y cmake gcc-c++ git libcurl-devel python3-pip</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will install:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>cmake</code> - Build system generator</li>
<li><code>gcc-c++</code> - C++ compiler</li>
<li><code>git</code> - Version control (for cloning llama.cpp)</li>
<li><code>libcurl-devel</code> - CURL library (required by llama.cpp)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 9.1: Clone and Build llama.cpp</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Inside the ROCm container:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd ~
git clone https://github.com/ggerganov/llama.cpp.git
cd llama.cpp

# Build with rocWMMA support
cmake -B build -S . \
  -DGGML_HIP=ON \
  -DAMDGPU_TARGETS=&quot;gfx1151&quot; \
  -DGGML_HIP_ROCWMMA_FATTN=ON

cmake --build build --config Release -j$(nproc)"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span>
git clone https://github.com/ggerganov/llama.cpp.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> llama.cpp

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Build with rocWMMA support</span>
cmake -B build -S <span class="pl-c1">.</span> \
  -DGGML_HIP=ON \
  -DAMDGPU_TARGETS=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gfx1151<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -DGGML_HIP_ROCWMMA_FATTN=ON

cmake --build build --config Release -j<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>nproc<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE:</strong> The build process will take several minutes. You'll see compilation progress for GPU kernels and CPU code.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 9.2: Install Build</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Binaries will be in build/bin/
ls -lh build/bin/"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Binaries will be in build/bin/</span>
ls -lh build/bin/</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 10: Download Models and Test</h2><a id="user-content-phase-10-download-models-and-test" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 10: Download Models and Test" href="#phase-10-download-models-and-test"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

  --image docker.io/kyuz0/amd-strix-halo-toolboxes:vulkan-radv \
  --additional-flags &quot;--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render&quot;

  --additional-flags &quot;--device /dev/dri --device /dev/kfd --group-add video --group-add render&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> RADV (most stable)</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Critical Reminders</h2><a id="user-content-critical-reminders" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Critical Reminders" href="#critical-reminders"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Always use <code>--no-mmap</code></strong> flag with llama.cpp on GPU backends</li>
<li><strong>Always use <code>--ngl 99</code></strong> (or 999) to offload all layers to GPU</li>
<li><strong>Store models in ~/models</strong> (outside containers) to persist across updates</li>
<li><strong>Never use Ollama</strong> - it lacks proper Vulkan/AMD support</li>
<li><strong>Kernel 6.16.9+</strong> is critical for &gt;15GB VRAM access</li>
<li><strong>Don't change VRAM allocation at OS level</strong> after BIOS setup</li>
<li><strong>Set <code>ROCBLAS_USE_HIPBLASLT=1</code></strong> environment variable (already set in kyuz0 containers)</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Expectations</h2><a id="user-content-performance-expectations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Expectations" href="#performance-expectations"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Llama-2-7B</strong>: ~50-52 tokens/second (similar to Apple M4 Max)</li>
<li><strong>Prompt processing with rocWMMA</strong>: 2× faster than Vulkan at BF16</li>
<li><strong>Long context (8K+ tokens)</strong>: ROCm rocWMMA excels (51 t/s vs Vulkan's 32 t/s)</li>
<li><strong>Memory bandwidth</strong>: ~212 GB/s internal, ~84 GB/s CPU-to-GPU</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Troubleshooting Quick Reference</h2><a id="user-content-troubleshooting-quick-reference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Troubleshooting Quick Reference" href="#troubleshooting-quick-reference"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Ubuntu-Specific Issues</h3><a id="user-content-ubuntu-specific-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Ubuntu-Specific Issues" href="#ubuntu-specific-issues"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>toolbox</code> package not found</strong>: Ubuntu 24.04 doesn't include <code>toolbox</code> in repos. Use <code>distrobox</code> instead (see Phase 6)</li>
<li><strong><code>HSA_STATUS_ERROR_OUT_OF_RESOURCES</code> when running <code>rocminfo</code></strong>: Missing renderD udev rule. Ensure <code>/etc/udev/rules.d/99-amd-kfd.rules</code> includes the <code>renderD[0-9]*</code> rule (see Step 4.1), then reload with <code>sudo udevadm control --reload-rules &amp;&amp; sudo udevadm trigger</code></li>
<li><strong>Container can't access GPU</strong>: Verify device permissions with <code>ls -la /dev/kfd /dev/dri/</code>. All should be <code>0666</code> (crw-rw-rw-)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Build Issues in Container</h3><a id="user-content-build-issues-in-container" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Build Issues in Container" href="#build-issues-in-container"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>cmake: command not found</code></strong>: The ROCm container doesn't include build tools. Install them with <code>sudo dnf install -y cmake gcc-c++ git libcurl-devel</code> (see Step 9.0)</li>
<li><strong><code>Could NOT find CURL</code> error during cmake</strong>: Install libcurl-devel with <code>sudo dnf install -y libcurl-devel</code></li>
<li><strong>Container uses <code>dnf</code> not <code>apt</code></strong>: The ROCm container is Fedora-based. Use <code>dnf</code> for package management, not <code>apt</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">llama.cpp Runtime Issues</h3><a id="user-content-llamacpp-runtime-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: llama.cpp Runtime Issues" href="#llamacpp-runtime-issues"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>error: invalid argument: --ngl</code></strong>: Use <code>-ngl</code> (single dash) not <code>--ngl</code> (double dash) for GPU layer offloading</li>
<li><strong><code>error: invalid parameter for argument: --no-mmap</code></strong> (llama-bench): Use <code>-mmp 0</code> or <code>--mmap 0</code> instead. The <code>--no-mmap</code> flag only works with <code>llama-cli</code>, not <code>llama-bench</code></li>
<li><strong><code>hf: command not found</code></strong>: The HuggingFace CLI changed to <code>hf download</code> instead of <code>huggingface-cli download</code>. If using pyenv, use full path: <code>~/.pyenv/versions/3.14.0/bin/hf</code></li>
<li><strong>Square brackets error in zsh</strong> (<code>huggingface-hub[cli]</code>): Quote the package name: <code>pip install "huggingface-hub[cli]"</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">General Issues</h3><a id="user-content-general-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: General Issues" href="#general-issues"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Permission denied on GPU</strong>: Check udev rules in Phase 4 and verify user is in <code>video</code> and <code>render</code> groups</li>
<li><strong>Only 15.5GB VRAM visible</strong>: Upgrade kernel to 6.16.9+</li>
<li><strong>Slow model loading</strong>: Add <code>--no-mmap</code> flag</li>
<li><strong>ROCm crashes</strong>: Try Vulkan RADV backend instead</li>
<li><strong>Poor performance</strong>: Verify <code>tuned-adm active</code> shows accelerator-performance</li>
<li><strong>Confused about VRAM vs GTT</strong>: For APUs, GTT (128GB) is what matters for compute, not VRAM (1GB). This is normal and expected.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Next Steps After Setup</h2><a id="user-content-next-steps-after-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Next Steps After Setup" href="#next-steps-after-setup"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Once you have completed this roadmap and verified that everything works:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Benchmark multiple backends</strong> (ROCm 7 RC rocWMMA, Vulkan RADV, Vulkan AMDVLK) with your specific workloads</li>
<li><strong>Test with different model sizes</strong> to find optimal configurations for your 120GB VRAM</li>
<li><strong>Explore long-context scenarios</strong> where ROCm rocWMMA significantly outperforms Vulkan</li>
<li><strong>Monitor kernel updates</strong> as gfx1151 support continues to mature</li>
<li><strong>Consider TheRock nightly builds</strong> for bleeding-edge performance improvements</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">This roadmap gives you a production-ready setup for ROCm 7 RC with rocWMMA and hipBLASlt on your GMKTEC EVO-X2. The container-based approach ensures reproducibility and easy updates as ROCm support for gfx1151 continues maturing.</p>
